   321	def transform_record(raw, item):
   322	    e, de, dde = (np.asarray(raw[name], dtype=float) for name in ("coframe", "coframe_first", "coframe_second"))
   323	    g, dg, ddg = (np.asarray(raw[name], dtype=float) for name in ("metric", "metric_first", "metric_second"))
   324	    riemann, weyl, ricci = (np.asarray(raw[name], dtype=float) for name in ("riemann_down", "weyl_down", "ricci"))
   325	    scalar = float(raw["observables"]["scalar_curvature"])
   326	    base_cartan = cartan_curvature(e, g, riemann)
   327	    if item["kind"] == "COORDINATE":
   328	        j = item["matrix"]
   329	        et, det, ddet = transform_coframe_coordinate(e, de, dde, j)
   330	        gt, dgt, ddgt = transform_metric_coordinate(g, dg, ddg, j)
   331	        rt, wt, rit = transform_covariant4(riemann, j), transform_covariant4(weyl, j), transform_covariant2(ricci, j)
   332	        phiv, phid, phidd = transform_phi(raw["phi"], j)
   333	        predicted_cartan = np.einsum("ua,vb,ijuv->ijab", j, j, base_cartan)
   334	        roundtrip = transform_metric_coordinate(gt, dgt, ddgt, np.linalg.inv(j))
   335	        roundtrip_residual = max(relmax(roundtrip[0], g), relmax(roundtrip[1], dg), relmax(roundtrip[2], ddg))
   336	        determinant_expected = np.linalg.det(j) ** 2 * np.linalg.det(g)
   337	    else:
   338	        et, det, ddet = transform_coframe_internal(e, de, dde, item)
   339	        gt, dgt, ddgt = g.copy(), dg.copy(), ddg.copy()
   340	        rt, wt, rit = riemann.copy(), weyl.copy(), ricci.copy()
   341	        phiv, phid, phidd = transform_phi(raw["phi"], np.eye(4))
   342	        lam = item["matrix"]
   343	        predicted_cartan = np.einsum("ia,abuv,bj->ijuv", lam, base_cartan, np.linalg.inv(lam))
   344	        roundtrip_residual = 0.0
   345	        determinant_expected = np.linalg.det(g)
   346	    metric_from_frame = metric_from_coframe(et, det, ddet)
   347	    metric_residual = max(relmax(metric_from_frame[0], gt), relmax(metric_from_frame[1], dgt), relmax(metric_from_frame[2], ddgt))
   348	    ct = cartan_curvature(et, gt, rt)
   349	    cartan_residual = relmax(ct, predicted_cartan)
   350	    inverse = np.linalg.inv(gt)
   351	    up = np.einsum("ra,asuv->rsuv", inverse, rt)
   352	    ricci_from_riemann = np.einsum("rsrn->sn", up)
   353	    scalar_from_ricci = float(np.einsum("ab,ab", inverse, rit))
   354	    split = split_from_metric_jets(gt, dgt, ddgt)
   355	    payload = {
   356	        "metric_twojet": flatten_twojet(gt, dgt, ddgt), "riemann": rt.reshape(-1),
   357	        "weyl": wt.reshape(-1), "ricci": rit.reshape(-1), "scalar": np.array([scalar]),
   358	        "cartan_curvature": ct.reshape(-1), "phi_twojet": flatten_twojet(phiv, phid, phidd),
   359	        "split_slot_twojet": None, "split_shear": None, "split_twist": None,
   360	    }
   361	    if split["status"] == "DEFINED":
   362	        payload.update({
   363	            "split_slot_twojet": flatten_twojet(split["values"], split["first"], split["second"]),
   364	            "split_shear": split["shear"].reshape(-1), "split_twist": split["twist"].reshape(-1),
   365	        })
   366	    determinant_residual = abs(float(np.linalg.det(gt)) - determinant_expected) / max(1.0, abs(determinant_expected))
   367	    ricci_residual = relmax(ricci_from_riemann, rit)
   368	    scalar_residual = abs(scalar_from_ricci - scalar) / max(1.0, abs(scalar))
   369	    weyl_trace = float(np.max(np.abs(np.einsum("ac,abcd->bd", inverse, wt))))
   370	    failures = max(metric_residual, cartan_residual, determinant_residual, ricci_residual, scalar_residual, roundtrip_residual)
   371	    if failures > TOL:
   372	        primary = "NUMERIC_COVARIANCE_FAILURE"
   373	    elif item["kind"] == "COFRAME":
   374	        primary = "METRIC_INVARIANT_COFRAME_GAUGE"
   375	    elif split["status"] == "INVALID_SIGNATURE":
   376	        primary = "SUPPLIED_SPLIT_UNDEFINED_SIGNATURE"
   377	    elif split["status"] == "MARGINAL":
   378	        primary = "SUPPLIED_SPLIT_MARGINAL"
   379	    elif item["distribution"] in {"CROSS_RESEATED", "PERMUTED_RESEATED"}:
   380	        primary = "SUPPLIED_SPLIT_RESEATED_DEFINED"
   381	    else:
   382	        primary = "TENSOR_COVARIANT_COMPONENT_CHANGE"
   383	    return payload, split, {
   384	        "primary_status": primary, "metric_twojet_residual": metric_residual,
   385	        "cartan_covariance_residual": cartan_residual, "determinant_weight_residual": determinant_residual,
   386	        "ricci_contraction_residual": ricci_residual, "scalar_contraction_residual": scalar_residual,
   387	        "weyl_trace_max_abs": weyl_trace, "inverse_roundtrip_residual": roundtrip_residual,
   388	        "metric_determinant": float(np.linalg.det(gt)),
   389	        "metric_inertia": ",".join(map(str, inertia(gt))),
   390	    }
   391	
   392	
   393	def inertia(matrix):
   394	    eigs = np.linalg.eigvalsh(matrix)
   395	    return int(np.count_nonzero(eigs < -ACTIVE_TOL)), int(np.count_nonzero(eigs > ACTIVE_TOL)), int(np.count_nonzero(np.abs(eigs) <= ACTIVE_TOL))
   396	
   397	
   398	def represent_payload(name: str, vector: np.ndarray, item):
   399	    if item["kind"] == "COFRAME":
   400	        if name == "cartan_curvature":
   401	            c = vector.reshape(4, 4, 4, 4)
   402	            lam = item["matrix"]
   403	            return np.einsum("ia,abuv,bj->ijuv", lam, c, np.linalg.inv(lam)).reshape(-1)
   404	        return vector.copy()
   405	    j = item["matrix"]
   406	    if name == "metric_twojet":
   407	        g, dg, ddg = vector[:16].reshape(4, 4), vector[16:80].reshape(4, 4, 4), vector[80:].reshape(4, 4, 4, 4)
   408	        return flatten_twojet(*transform_metric_coordinate(g, dg, ddg, j))
   409	    if name in {"riemann", "weyl"}:
   410	        return transform_covariant4(vector.reshape(4, 4, 4, 4), j).reshape(-1)
   411	    if name == "ricci":
   412	        return transform_covariant2(vector.reshape(4, 4), j).reshape(-1)
   413	    if name == "scalar":
   414	        return vector.copy()
   415	    if name == "cartan_curvature":
   416	        return np.einsum("ua,vb,ijuv->ijab", j, j, vector.reshape(4, 4, 4, 4)).reshape(-1)
   417	    if name == "phi_twojet":
   418	        return flatten_twojet(np.array([vector[0]]), np.einsum("ka,k->a", j, vector[1:5]), np.einsum("ka,lb,kl->ab", j, j, vector[5:].reshape(4, 4)))
   419	    if item["id"] == "C00_IDENTITY":
   420	        return vector.copy()
   421	    return None
   422	
   423	
   424	def interaction_fields() -> list[str]:
   425	    fields = ["transform_id", "interaction_id", "carrier_id", "bank", "point_id", "target_mask", "target_integer", "ensemble_order", "subsets_used"]
   426	    for name in PAYLOADS:
   427	        fields.extend([f"{name}_domain", f"{name}_l2", f"{name}_max_abs", f"{name}_active", f"{name}_baseline_active", f"{name}_covariance_residual"])
   428	    return fields
   429	
   430	
   431	def main() -> None:
   432	    checks = []
   433	
   434	    def check(name, condition):
   435	        if not condition:
   436	            raise AssertionError(name)
   437	        checks.append(name)
   438	
   439	    PREREG_HASHES["PREREGISTRATION_CORRECTION.md"] = "c3ee82ce5603a8bfeabc653e56ab8664b17f1c7597ddfa9ec0a3fa69cc948454"
   440	    for path, expected in SOURCE_HASHES.items():
   441	        check(f"source_{path}", digest(ROOT / path) == expected)
   442	    for path, expected in PREREG_HASHES.items():
   443	        check(f"prereg_{path}", digest(HERE / path) == expected)
   444	    source_rows = [{"path": path, "sha256": value, "role": "IMMUTABLE_SOURCE"} for path, value in SOURCE_HASHES.items()]
   445	    source_rows += [{"path": path, "sha256": value, "role": "PREREGISTRATION"} for path, value in PREREG_HASHES.items()]
   446	    write_tsv("SOURCE_LINEAGE.tsv", ["path", "sha256", "role"], source_rows)
   447	
   448	    transforms = coordinate_matrices() + coframe_transforms()
   449	    check("transformation_count", len(transforms) == 12 and len({x["id"] for x in transforms}) == 12)
   450	    transform_rows = []
   451	    for item in transforms:
   452	        matrix = item["matrix"]
   453	        lorentz_residual = relmax(matrix.T @ ETA @ matrix, ETA) if item["kind"] == "COFRAME" else ""
   454	        check(f"invertible_{item['id']}", abs(np.linalg.det(matrix)) > 1e-12)
   455	        if item["kind"] == "COFRAME":
   456	            check(f"lorentz_{item['id']}", float(lorentz_residual) <= TOL)
   457	        transform_rows.append({
   458	            "transform_id": item["id"], "kind": item["kind"], "distribution_relation": item["distribution"],
   459	            "inverse_pair": item["inverse_pair"], "determinant": float(np.linalg.det(matrix)),
   460	            "matrix_json": json.dumps(matrix.tolist(), separators=(",", ":")),
   461	            "local": "YES" if item.get("local", False) else "NO",
   462	            "generator": item.get("generator", ""), "parameter": item.get("parameter", ""),
   463	            "parameter_first_json": json.dumps(np.asarray(item.get("parameter_first", [])).tolist(), separators=(",", ":")),
   464	            "parameter_second_json": json.dumps(np.asarray(item.get("parameter_second", [])).tolist(), separators=(",", ":")),
   465	            "lorentz_residual": lorentz_residual,
   466	        })
   467	    write_tsv("TRANSFORMATION_REGISTRY.tsv", list(transform_rows[0]), transform_rows)
   468	
   469	    parent_config = read_tsv(PARENT / "CONFIGURATION_OBSERVATIONS.tsv")
   470	    parent_interactions = read_tsv(PARENT / "MOBIUS_INTERACTIONS.tsv")
   471	    check("parent_configurations", len(parent_config) == 6144 and len({r["configuration_id"] for r in parent_config}) == 6144)
   472	    check("parent_interactions", len(parent_interactions) == 5760 and len({r["interaction_id"] for r in parent_interactions}) == 5760)
   473	    shard_registry = read_tsv(PARENT / "RAW_SHARD_REGISTRY.tsv")
   474	    check("parent_raw_shards", len(shard_registry) == 8 and sum(int(r["records"]) for r in shard_registry) == 6144)
   475	
   476	    config_fields = [
   477	        "transform_id", "configuration_id", "carrier_id", "mask_id", "mask_integer", "bank", "point_id",
   478	        "primary_status", "split_status", "q_eigenvalues", "h_eigenvalues", "split_forward_residual",
   479	        "shear_rank", "twist_rank", "shear_max_abs", "twist_max_abs", "metric_twojet_residual",
   480	        "cartan_covariance_residual", "determinant_weight_residual", "ricci_contraction_residual",

 succeeded in 0ms:
   481	        "scalar_contraction_residual", "weyl_trace_max_abs", "inverse_roundtrip_residual",
   482	        "metric_determinant", "metric_inertia", "retained", "physical_merit",
   483	    ]
   484	    interaction_header = interaction_fields()
   485	    config_handles, config_writers, interaction_handles, interaction_writers = {}, {}, {}, {}
   486	    config_shards, interaction_shards = [], []
   487	    for item in transforms:
   488	        identity = item["id"]
   489	        cp = HERE / f"CONFIGURATION_ORBITS_{identity}.tsv"
   490	        mp = HERE / f"MOBIUS_ORBITS_{identity}.tsv"
   491	        config_handles[identity] = cp.open("w", encoding="utf-8", newline="")
   492	        interaction_handles[identity] = mp.open("w", encoding="utf-8", newline="")
   493	        config_writers[identity] = csv.DictWriter(config_handles[identity], fieldnames=config_fields, delimiter="\t", lineterminator="\n")
   494	        interaction_writers[identity] = csv.DictWriter(interaction_handles[identity], fieldnames=interaction_header, delimiter="\t", lineterminator="\n")
   495	        config_writers[identity].writeheader()
   496	        interaction_writers[identity].writeheader()
   497	
   498	    config_status = defaultdict(Counter)
   499	    split_status = defaultdict(Counter)
   500	    order_stats = defaultdict(lambda: Counter())
   501	    margins = defaultdict(list)
   502	    span_vectors = defaultdict(list)
   503	    max_residuals = defaultdict(float)
   504	    config_counts = Counter()
   505	    interaction_counts = Counter()
   506	
   507	    for shard in shard_registry:
   508	        with (PARENT / shard["path"]).open(encoding="utf-8") as handle:
   509	            raw_rows = [json.loads(line) for line in handle]
   510	        check(f"raw_shard_{shard['path']}", len(raw_rows) == int(shard["records"]) and digest(PARENT / shard["path"]) == shard["sha256"])
   511	        transformed_context = {item["id"]: {} for item in transforms}
   512	        baseline_context = {}
   513	        for raw in raw_rows:
   514	            key = (raw["carrier_id"], int(raw["mask_integer"]))
   515	            baseline_context[key] = baseline_payload(raw)
   516	            for item in transforms:
   517	                identity = item["id"]
   518	                payload, split, diagnostics = transform_record(raw, item)
   519	                transformed_context[identity][key] = payload
   520	                q_eigs, h_eigs = split["q_eigs"], split["h_eigs"]
   521	                row = {
   522	                    "transform_id": identity, "configuration_id": raw["configuration_id"], "carrier_id": raw["carrier_id"],
   523	                    "mask_id": raw["mask_id"], "mask_integer": raw["mask_integer"], "bank": raw["bank"], "point_id": raw["point_id"],
   524	                    **diagnostics, "split_status": split["status"],
   525	                    "q_eigenvalues": ";".join(f"{x:.17g}" for x in q_eigs),
   526	                    "h_eigenvalues": ";".join("nan" if not np.isfinite(x) else f"{x:.17g}" for x in h_eigs),
   527	                    "split_forward_residual": split.get("forward_residual", ""),
   528	                    "shear_rank": int(np.linalg.matrix_rank(split["shear"], tol=ACTIVE_TOL)) if split["status"] == "DEFINED" else "",
   529	                    "twist_rank": int(np.linalg.matrix_rank(split["twist"].reshape(2, 1), tol=ACTIVE_TOL)) if split["status"] == "DEFINED" else "",
   530	                    "shear_max_abs": float(np.max(np.abs(split["shear"]))) if split["status"] == "DEFINED" else "",
   531	                    "twist_max_abs": float(np.max(np.abs(split["twist"]))) if split["status"] == "DEFINED" else "",
   532	                    "retained": "YES", "physical_merit": "NOT_EVALUATED",
   533	                }
   534	                config_writers[identity].writerow(row)
   535	                config_counts[identity] += 1
   536	                config_status[identity][diagnostics["primary_status"]] += 1
   537	                split_status[identity][split["status"]] += 1
   538	                for field in ("metric_twojet_residual", "cartan_covariance_residual", "determinant_weight_residual", "ricci_contraction_residual", "scalar_contraction_residual", "inverse_roundtrip_residual"):
   539	                    max_residuals[(identity, field)] = max(max_residuals[(identity, field)], float(diagnostics[field]))
   540	
   541	        carrier_ids = sorted({r["carrier_id"] for r in raw_rows})
   542	        bank, point_id = raw_rows[0]["bank"], raw_rows[0]["point_id"]
   543	        for item in transforms:
   544	            identity = item["id"]
   545	            for carrier in carrier_ids:
   546	                for target in range(1, 16):
   547	                    subsets = [subset for subset in range(16) if subset & ~target == 0]
   548	                    interaction_id = f"{carrier}_T{target:X}_{bank}_{point_id}"
   549	                    row = {
   550	                        "transform_id": identity, "interaction_id": interaction_id, "carrier_id": carrier,
   551	                        "bank": bank, "point_id": point_id, "target_mask": f"M{target:X}", "target_integer": target,
   552	                        "ensemble_order": target.bit_count(), "subsets_used": ";".join(f"M{x:X}" for x in subsets),
   553	                    }
   554	                    for name in PAYLOADS:
   555	                        base = sum(((-1) ** (target.bit_count() - subset.bit_count())) * baseline_context[(carrier, subset)][name] for subset in subsets)
   556	                        vertices = [transformed_context[identity][(carrier, subset)][name] for subset in subsets]
   557	                        base_active = "YES" if float(np.max(np.abs(base))) > ACTIVE_TOL else "NO"
   558	                        if any(value is None for value in vertices):
   559	                            row.update({f"{name}_domain": "UNDEFINED_SPLIT_DOMAIN", f"{name}_l2": "", f"{name}_max_abs": "", f"{name}_active": "", f"{name}_baseline_active": base_active, f"{name}_covariance_residual": ""})
   560	                            order_stats[(identity, target.bit_count(), name)]["undefined"] += 1
   561	                            continue
   562	                        vector = sum(((-1) ** (target.bit_count() - subset.bit_count())) * vertices[index] for index, subset in enumerate(subsets))
   563	                        maximum = float(np.max(np.abs(vector)))
   564	                        active = "YES" if maximum > ACTIVE_TOL else "NO"
   565	                        expected = represent_payload(name, base, item)
   566	                        covariance = relmax(vector, expected) if expected is not None else ""
   567	                        domain = "DEFINED_COVARIANCE_CHECKED" if expected is not None else "DEFINED_NO_LINEAR_CONTRACT"
   568	                        row.update({f"{name}_domain": domain, f"{name}_l2": float(np.linalg.norm(vector)), f"{name}_max_abs": maximum, f"{name}_active": active, f"{name}_baseline_active": base_active, f"{name}_covariance_residual": covariance})
   569	                        span_vectors[(identity, target, name)].append(vector)
   570	                        margins[(identity, name)].append(maximum)
   571	                        order_stats[(identity, target.bit_count(), name)]["defined"] += 1
   572	                        order_stats[(identity, target.bit_count(), name)]["active" if active == "YES" else "inactive"] += 1
   573	                        order_stats[(identity, target.bit_count(), name)]["discordant" if active != base_active else "concordant"] += 1
   574	                        if covariance != "":
   575	                            max_residuals[(identity, f"mobius_{name}")] = max(max_residuals[(identity, f"mobius_{name}")], float(covariance))
   576	                    interaction_writers[identity].writerow(row)
   577	                    interaction_counts[identity] += 1
   578	
   579	    for handle in list(config_handles.values()) + list(interaction_handles.values()):
   580	        handle.close()
   581	    for item in transforms:
   582	        identity = item["id"]
   583	        cp, mp = HERE / f"CONFIGURATION_ORBITS_{identity}.tsv", HERE / f"MOBIUS_ORBITS_{identity}.tsv"
   584	        config_shards.append({"transform_id": identity, "path": cp.name, "rows": config_counts[identity], "bytes": cp.stat().st_size, "sha256": digest(cp)})
   585	        interaction_shards.append({"transform_id": identity, "path": mp.name, "rows": interaction_counts[identity], "bytes": mp.stat().st_size, "sha256": digest(mp)})
   586	    check("configuration_orbit_count", sum(config_counts.values()) == 73728 and all(value == 6144 for value in config_counts.values()))
   587	    check("interaction_orbit_count", sum(interaction_counts.values()) == 69120 and all(value == 5760 for value in interaction_counts.values()))
   588	    check("no_numeric_covariance_failures", sum(c["NUMERIC_COVARIANCE_FAILURE"] for c in config_status.values()) == 0)
   589	    check("full_tensor_mobius_covariance", all(value <= TOL for (identity, field), value in max_residuals.items() if field.startswith("mobius_") and field.replace("mobius_", "") not in SPLIT_PAYLOADS))
   590	    check("all_retained", sum(config_counts.values()) == 73728)
   591	    write_tsv("CONFIGURATION_ORBIT_SHARDS.tsv", list(config_shards[0]), config_shards)
   592	    write_tsv("MOBIUS_ORBIT_SHARDS.tsv", list(interaction_shards[0]), interaction_shards)
   593	
   594	    census_rows = []
   595	    split_rows = []
   596	    for item in transforms:
   597	        identity = item["id"]
   598	        for status, count in sorted(config_status[identity].items()):
   599	            census_rows.append({"transform_id": identity, "kind": item["kind"], "primary_status": status, "configurations": count})
   600	        for status, count in sorted(split_status[identity].items()):
   601	            split_rows.append({"transform_id": identity, "distribution_relation": item["distribution"], "split_status": status, "configurations": count, "retained": "YES"})
   602	    write_tsv("INVARIANCE_CENSUS.tsv", list(census_rows[0]), census_rows)
   603	    write_tsv("SPLIT_DOMAIN_CENSUS.tsv", list(split_rows[0]), split_rows)
   604	
   605	    order_rows = []
   606	    for (identity, order, name), counter in sorted(order_stats.items()):
   607	        order_rows.append({"transform_id": identity, "ensemble_order": order, "payload": name, "defined_rows": counter["defined"], "undefined_rows": counter["undefined"], "active_rows": counter["active"], "inactive_rows": counter["inactive"], "activity_concordant": counter["concordant"], "activity_discordant": counter["discordant"]})
   608	    write_tsv("INTERACTION_ORDER_CENSUS.tsv", list(order_rows[0]), order_rows)
   609	
   610	    span_rows = []
   611	    for item in transforms:
   612	        identity = item["id"]
   613	        for target in range(1, 16):
   614	            for name in PAYLOADS:
   615	                vectors = span_vectors[(identity, target, name)]
   616	                if vectors:
   617	                    matrix = np.stack(vectors)
   618	                    singular = np.linalg.svd(matrix, compute_uv=False)
   619	                    rank = int(np.count_nonzero(singular > ACTIVE_TOL))
   620	                    retained = singular[singular > ACTIVE_TOL]
   621	                    discarded = singular[singular <= ACTIVE_TOL]
   622	                    row = {"vectors_defined": len(vectors), "components": matrix.shape[1], "span_rank": rank, "largest_singular": float(singular[0]), "min_retained_singular": float(np.min(retained)) if retained.size else 0.0, "max_discarded_singular": float(np.max(discarded)) if discarded.size else 0.0}
   623	                else:
   624	                    row = {"vectors_defined": 0, "components": "", "span_rank": "", "largest_singular": "", "min_retained_singular": "", "max_discarded_singular": ""}
   625	                span_rows.append({"transform_id": identity, "target_mask": f"M{target:X}", "target_integer": target, "ensemble_order": target.bit_count(), "payload": name, **row, "rank_threshold": ACTIVE_TOL, "physical_dof_claimed": "NO"})
   626	    check("span_rows", len(span_rows) == 1800)
   627	    write_tsv("TRANSFORMED_SPAN_RANKS.tsv", list(span_rows[0]), span_rows)
   628	
   629	    margin_rows = []
   630	    for item in transforms:
   631	        identity = item["id"]
   632	        for name in PAYLOADS:
   633	            values = margins[(identity, name)]
   634	            active = [v for v in values if v > ACTIVE_TOL]
   635	            inactive = [v for v in values if v <= ACTIVE_TOL]
   636	            margin_rows.append({"transform_id": identity, "payload": name, "defined_rows": len(values), "active_rows": len(active), "inactive_rows": len(inactive), "uncertain_rows": sum(MARGIN_LOW <= v <= MARGIN_HIGH for v in values), "min_active_max_abs": min(active) if active else 0.0, "max_inactive_max_abs": max(inactive) if inactive else 0.0, "max_observed_abs": max(values) if values else "", "activity_threshold": ACTIVE_TOL})
   637	    write_tsv("NUMERIC_MARGIN_LEDGER.tsv", list(margin_rows[0]), margin_rows)
   638	
   639	    residual_rows = [{"transform_id": identity, "quantity": field, "max_relative_residual": value, "tolerance": TOL, "pass": "YES" if value <= TOL else "NO"} for (identity, field), value in sorted(max_residuals.items())]
   640	    write_tsv("COVARIANCE_RESIDUAL_CENSUS.tsv", list(residual_rows[0]), residual_rows)
   641	
   642	    coverage = [
   643	        ("C01", "parent configurations", 6144, 6144), ("C02", "parent interactions", 5760, 5760),
   644	        ("C03", "registered transformations", 12, 12), ("C04", "configuration orbit rows", sum(config_counts.values()), 73728),
   645	        ("C05", "interaction orbit rows", sum(interaction_counts.values()), 69120), ("C06", "configuration shards", len(config_shards), 12),
   646	        ("C07", "interaction shards", len(interaction_shards), 12), ("C08", "span rows", len(span_rows), 1800),
   647	        ("C09", "discarded configurations", 0, 0), ("C10", "solutions/actions loaded", 0, 0),
   648	    ]
   649	    write_tsv("COVERAGE_LEDGER.tsv", ["id", "object", "observed", "required", "pass"], [{"id": a, "object": b, "observed": c, "required": d, "pass": "YES" if c == d else "NO"} for a, b, c, d in coverage])
   650	    premise_rows = [
   651	        ("P01", "4D conformal-Lorentzian coframe metric", "CONDITIONAL", "parent realization"),
   652	        ("P02", "twelve exact transformations", "FREE_AND_EXPLORED", "finite registered probes"),
   653	        ("P03", "constant coordinate charts", "BOUNDED", "nonlinear charts open"),
   654	        ("P04", "local Lorentz coframes", "GAUGE_TEST", "registered values and two-jets"),
   655	        ("P05", "first-two last-two split", "CHOSE", "reseated and audited, not selected"),
   656	        ("P06", "ensemble mask histories", "CHOSE", "fixed before transformations"),
   657	        ("P07", "component activity threshold", "PINNED_BY_HABIT", "1e-9 with margins"),
   658	        ("P08", "action source carrier boundary scale", "OPEN", "not loaded"),
   659	    ]
   660	    write_tsv("PREMISE_STATUS_LEDGER.tsv", ["id", "premise", "status", "scope"], [{"id": a, "premise": b, "status": c, "scope": d} for a, b, c, d in premise_rows])
   661	    anti = [
   662	        "chart component change called new geometry", "coframe gauge called physical sector", "reseated split called selected",
   663	        "invalid split discarded", "undefined split imputed", "component rank called physical degrees of freedom",
   664	        "ensemble mask re-fit after transform", "finite probes called full group proof", "action or source inferred",
   665	        "unexpected pattern filtered", "coordinate reseating called evolution", "physical merit ranking",
   666	    ]
   667	    write_tsv("ANTI_IMPOSITION_AUDIT.tsv", ["id", "failure_mode", "present"], [{"id": f"A{i:02d}", "failure_mode": text, "present": "ABSENT"} for i, text in enumerate(anti, 1)])
   668	
   669	    result = {
   670	        "schema": SCHEMA, "status": "PASS", "classification": CLASSIFICATION, "maximum_conclusion": MAXIMUM,
   671	        "checks": len(checks), "checks_passed": checks, "transformations": len(transforms),
   672	        "configuration_records": 6144, "interaction_records": 5760,
   673	        "configuration_orbit_records": sum(config_counts.values()), "interaction_orbit_records": sum(interaction_counts.values()),
   674	        "configuration_shards": len(config_shards), "interaction_shards": len(interaction_shards), "span_rows": len(span_rows),
   675	        "split_domain_counts": {identity: dict(counter) for identity, counter in sorted(split_status.items())},
   676	        "primary_status_counts": {identity: dict(counter) for identity, counter in sorted(config_status.items())},
   677	        "max_certification_residual": max(max_residuals.values()),
   678	        "numeric_covariance_failures": sum(c["NUMERIC_COVARIANCE_FAILURE"] for c in config_status.values()),
   679	        "discarded_records": 0, "physical_merit_filter": False, "action_loaded": False, "solutions_run": 0,
   680	        "full_group_exhaustiveness_claim": False, "split_selected_claim": False, "gpu_used": False,
   681	        "evidence_grade": "OBSERVED_PENDING_INDEPENDENT_VERIFICATION",
   682	    }
   683	    (HERE / "ATLAS_RESULT.json").write_text(json.dumps(result, indent=2, sort_keys=True) + "\n", encoding="utf-8")

   393	def inertia(matrix):
   394	    eigs = np.linalg.eigvalsh(matrix)

    41	def digest(path: Path) -> str:
    42	    value = hashlib.sha256()
    43	    with path.open("rb") as handle:
    44	        for block in iter(lambda: handle.read(131072), b""):
    45	            value.update(block)
    46	    return value.hexdigest()

    61	def relmax(actual, expected) -> float:
    62	    a, b = np.asarray(actual, dtype=float), np.asarray(expected, dtype=float)
    63	    return float(np.max(np.abs(a - b)) / max(1.0, float(np.max(np.abs(b)))))

    66	def transform_metric(g, dg, ddg, j):
    67	    return (
    68	        np.einsum("ma,mn,nb->ab", j, g, j),
    69	        np.einsum("ka,mb,nc,kmn->abc", j, j, j, dg),
    70	        np.einsum("ka,lb,mc,nd,klmn->abcd", j, j, j, j, ddg),
    71	    )
    72	
    73	
    74	def transform_four(value, j):
    75	    return np.einsum("ra,sb,uc,vd,rsuv->abcd", j, j, j, j, value)

    78	def generator(name: str) -> np.ndarray:
    79	    k = np.zeros((4, 4))
    80	    if name == "K01":
    81	        k[0, 1] = k[1, 0] = 1.0
    82	    elif name == "K02":
    83	        k[0, 2] = k[2, 0] = 1.0
    84	    elif name == "K23":
    85	        k[2, 3], k[3, 2] = -1.0, 1.0
    86	    else:
    87	        raise ValueError(name)
    88	    return k

    91	def coframe_metric(e, de, dde):
    92	    g = e.T @ ETA @ e
    93	    dg = np.array([de[k].T @ ETA @ e + e.T @ ETA @ de[k] for k in range(4)])
    94	    ddg = np.array([[dde[k, l].T @ ETA @ e + de[k].T @ ETA @ de[l] + de[l].T @ ETA @ de[k] + e.T @ ETA @ dde[k, l] for l in range(4)] for k in range(4)])
    95	    return g, dg, ddg

    97	
    98	class D2:
    99	    """Independent scalar second-jet algebra used for the split check."""
   100	
   101	    def __init__(self, value, first=None, second=None):
   102	        self.v = float(value)
   103	        self.d = np.zeros(4) if first is None else np.asarray(first, dtype=float)
   104	        self.dd = np.zeros((4, 4)) if second is None else np.asarray(second, dtype=float)
   105	
   106	    def __add__(self, other):
   107	        b = other if isinstance(other, D2) else D2(other)
   108	        return D2(self.v + b.v, self.d + b.d, self.dd + b.dd)
   109	
   110	    __radd__ = __add__
   111	
   112	    def __neg__(self):
   113	        return D2(-self.v, -self.d, -self.dd)
   114	
   115	    def __sub__(self, other):
   116	        return self + (-other if isinstance(other, D2) else -other)
   117	
   118	    def __rsub__(self, other):
   119	        return (-self) + other
   120	
   121	    def __mul__(self, other):
   122	        b = other if isinstance(other, D2) else D2(other)
   123	        return D2(self.v * b.v, self.d * b.v + self.v * b.d, self.dd * b.v + self.v * b.dd + np.outer(self.d, b.d) + np.outer(b.d, self.d))
   124	
   125	    __rmul__ = __mul__
   126	
   127	    def reciprocal(self):
   128	        return D2(1.0 / self.v, -self.d / self.v**2, 2.0 * np.outer(self.d, self.d) / self.v**3 - self.dd / self.v**2)
   129	
   130	    def __truediv__(self, other):
   131	        b = other if isinstance(other, D2) else D2(other)
   132	        return self * b.reciprocal()
   133	
   134	
   135	def dmat(g, dg, ddg, row_slice, col_slice):
   136	    rs, cs = list(range(4))[row_slice], list(range(4))[col_slice]
   137	    return [[D2(g[i, j], dg[:, i, j], ddg[:, :, i, j]) for j in cs] for i in rs]
   138	
   139	
   140	def mmul(a, b):
   141	    return [[sum((a[i][k] * b[k][j] for k in range(len(b))), D2(0.0)) for j in range(len(b[0]))] for i in range(len(a))]
   142	
   143	
   144	def trans(a):
   145	    return [list(x) for x in zip(*a)]
   146	
   147	
   148	def independent_split(g, dg, ddg):
   149	    q = dmat(g, dg, ddg, slice(2, 4), slice(2, 4))
   150	    b = trans(dmat(g, dg, ddg, slice(0, 2), slice(2, 4)))
   151	    q_values = np.array([[q[i][j].v for j in range(2)] for i in range(2)])
   152	    qe = np.linalg.eigvalsh(q_values)
   153	    if np.min(np.abs(qe)) <= ACTIVE_TOL:
   154	        return {"status": "MARGINAL"}
   155	    determinant = q[0][0] * q[1][1] - q[0][1] * q[1][0]
   156	    qinv = [[q[1][1] / determinant, -q[0][1] / determinant], [-q[1][0] / determinant, q[0][0] / determinant]]
   157	    a = mmul(qinv, b)
   158	    correction = mmul(mmul(trans(b), qinv), b)
   159	    gbb = dmat(g, dg, ddg, slice(0, 2), slice(0, 2))
   160	    h = [[gbb[i][j] - correction[i][j] for j in range(2)] for i in range(2)]
   161	    h_values = np.array([[h[i][j].v for j in range(2)] for i in range(2)])
   162	    he = np.linalg.eigvalsh(h_values)
   163	    if np.min(np.abs(he)) <= ACTIVE_TOL:
   164	        return {"status": "MARGINAL"}
   165	    if not (np.all(qe > ACTIVE_TOL) and he[0] < -ACTIVE_TOL and he[1] > ACTIVE_TOL):
   166	        return {"status": "INVALID_SIGNATURE"}
   167	    jets = [h[0][0], h[0][1], h[1][1], q[0][0], q[0][1], q[1][1], a[0][0], a[1][0], a[0][1], a[1][1]]
   168	    values = np.array([x.v for x in jets])
   169	    first = np.array([x.d for x in jets]).T
   170	    second = np.transpose(np.array([x.dd for x in jets]), (1, 2, 0))
   171	    rebuilt = metric_jets_from_split(values, first, second)
   172	    forward = max(relmax(rebuilt.metric, g), relmax(rebuilt.first, dg), relmax(rebuilt.second, ddg))
   173	    shear, twist = independent_kinematics(values, first)
   174	    return {"status": "DEFINED", "values": values, "first": first, "second": second, "shear": shear, "twist": twist, "forward": forward}
   175	
   176	
   177	def independent_kinematics(values, first):
   178	    q = np.array([[values[3], values[4]], [values[4], values[5]]])
   179	    a = np.array([[values[6], values[8]], [values[7], values[9]]])
   180	    dq = np.array([[[first[k, 3], first[k, 4]], [first[k, 4], first[k, 5]]] for k in range(4)])
   181	    da = np.array([[[first[k, 6], first[k, 8]], [first[k, 7], first[k, 9]]] for k in range(4)])
   182	    twist = np.array([da[0, v, 1] - da[1, v, 0] - sum(a[o, 0] * da[2 + o, v, 1] for o in range(2)) + sum(a[o, 1] * da[2 + o, v, 0] for o in range(2)) for v in range(2)])
   183	    inverse = np.linalg.inv(q)
   184	    shears = []
   185	    for i in range(2):
   186	        horizontal = dq[i] - sum(a[v, i] * dq[2 + v] for v in range(2))
   187	        vertical = np.array([[da[2 + derivative, output, i] for output in range(2)] for derivative in range(2)])
   188	        deformation = 0.5 * (horizontal - vertical @ q - q @ vertical.T)
   189	        shear = deformation - 0.5 * np.trace(inverse @ deformation) * q
   190	        shears.append([shear[0, 0], shear[0, 1], shear[1, 1]])
   191	    return np.asarray(shears), twist
   192	
   193	
   194	def split_payload(split, name):
   195	    if split["status"] != "DEFINED":
   196	        return None
   197	    if name == "split_slot_twojet":
   198	        return np.concatenate((split["values"], split["first"].reshape(-1), split["second"].reshape(-1)))
   199	    if name == "split_shear":
   200	        return split["shear"].reshape(-1)
   201	    return split["twist"].reshape(-1)
   202	
   203	
   204	def must_fail(name, predicate, catch_rows):
   205	    failed = False
   206	    try:
   207	        failed = not bool(predicate())
   208	    except Exception:
   209	        failed = True
   210	    if not failed:
   211	        raise AssertionError(f"catch proof did not reject: {name}")
   212	    catch_rows.append({"catch_id": name, "result": "REJECTED_AS_REQUIRED"})
   213

   216	    checks: list[str] = []
   217	
   218	    def check(name, condition):
   219	        if not condition:
   220	            raise AssertionError(name)

     1	#!/usr/bin/env python3
     2	"""Law-neutral local 4D metric/coframe geometry evaluator for P01.
     3	
     4	The 2+2 interface is conditional on a supplied base/screen split.  Nothing in
     5	this module selects that split, an action, a source, or a physical solution.
     6	"""
     7	
     8	from __future__ import annotations
     9	
    10	from dataclasses import dataclass
    11	from typing import Iterable
    12	
    13	import numpy as np
    14	
    15	
    16	DIM = 4
    17	ETA = np.diag([-1.0, 1.0, 1.0, 1.0])
    18	SLOT_NAMES = (
    19	    "h00",
    20	    "h01",
    21	    "h11",
    22	    "q22",
    23	    "q23",
    24	    "q33",
    25	    "A2_0",
    26	    "A3_0",
    27	    "A2_1",
    28	    "A3_1",
    29	)
    30	
    31	
    32	class GeometryInputError(ValueError):
    33	    pass
    34	
    35	
    36	@dataclass(frozen=True)
    37	class MetricJets:
    38	    metric: np.ndarray
    39	    first: np.ndarray
    40	    second: np.ndarray
    41	
    42	
    43	@dataclass(frozen=True)
    44	class GeometryEvaluation:
    45	    metric: np.ndarray
    46	    inverse: np.ndarray
    47	    determinant: float
    48	    inertia: tuple[int, int, int]
    49	    christoffel: np.ndarray
    50	    christoffel_first: np.ndarray
    51	    riemann_up: np.ndarray
    52	    riemann_down: np.ndarray
    53	    ricci: np.ndarray
    54	    scalar_curvature: float
    55	    residuals: dict[str, float]
    56	
    57	
    58	@dataclass(frozen=True)
    59	class CoframeEvaluation:
    60	    metric_jets: MetricJets
    61	    geometry: GeometryEvaluation
    62	    inverse_frame: np.ndarray
    63	    spin_connection: np.ndarray
    64	    spin_connection_first: np.ndarray
    65	    torsion: np.ndarray
    66	    cartan_curvature: np.ndarray
    67	    coordinate_curvature_in_frame: np.ndarray
    68	    residuals: dict[str, float]
    69	
    70	
    71	@dataclass(frozen=True)
    72	class SplitReconstruction:
    73	    slots: np.ndarray
    74	    base: np.ndarray
    75	    screen: np.ndarray
    76	    shifts: np.ndarray
    77	    block_inverse: np.ndarray
    78	    determinant_factor: float
    79	    residuals: dict[str, float]
    80	
    81	
    82	@dataclass(frozen=True)
    83	class Jet2:
    84	    value: float
    85	    first: np.ndarray
    86	    second: np.ndarray
    87	
    88	    @classmethod
    89	    def constant(cls, value: float) -> "Jet2":
    90	        return cls(float(value), np.zeros(DIM), np.zeros((DIM, DIM)))
    91	
    92	    def __add__(self, other: float | "Jet2") -> "Jet2":
    93	        rhs = other if isinstance(other, Jet2) else Jet2.constant(float(other))
    94	        return Jet2(self.value + rhs.value, self.first + rhs.first, self.second + rhs.second)
    95	
    96	    __radd__ = __add__
    97	
    98	    def __neg__(self) -> "Jet2":
    99	        return Jet2(-self.value, -self.first, -self.second)
   100	
   101	    def __sub__(self, other: float | "Jet2") -> "Jet2":
   102	        return self + (-other if isinstance(other, Jet2) else -float(other))
   103	
   104	    def __rsub__(self, other: float | "Jet2") -> "Jet2":
   105	        return (-self) + other
   106	
   107	    def __mul__(self, other: float | "Jet2") -> "Jet2":
   108	        rhs = other if isinstance(other, Jet2) else Jet2.constant(float(other))
   109	        return Jet2(
   110	            self.value * rhs.value,
   111	            self.first * rhs.value + self.value * rhs.first,
   112	            self.second * rhs.value
   113	            + self.value * rhs.second
   114	            + np.outer(self.first, rhs.first)
   115	            + np.outer(rhs.first, self.first),
   116	        )
   117	
   118	    __rmul__ = __mul__
   119	
   120	
   121	def _as_float_array(value, shape: tuple[int, ...], name: str) -> np.ndarray:
   122	    array = np.asarray(value, dtype=float)
   123	    if array.shape != shape:
   124	        raise GeometryInputError(f"{name} shape {array.shape}, expected {shape}")
   125	    if not np.all(np.isfinite(array)):
   126	        raise GeometryInputError(f"{name} contains non-finite values")
   127	    return array
   128	
   129	
   130	def _maximum(array: np.ndarray) -> float:
   131	    return float(np.max(np.abs(array))) if array.size else 0.0
   132	
   133	
   134	def validate_metric_jets(jets: MetricJets, tolerance: float = 2e-10) -> MetricJets:
   135	    metric = _as_float_array(jets.metric, (DIM, DIM), "metric")
   136	    first = _as_float_array(jets.first, (DIM, DIM, DIM), "metric first jet")
   137	    second = _as_float_array(jets.second, (DIM, DIM, DIM, DIM), "metric second jet")
   138	    if _maximum(metric - metric.T) > tolerance:
   139	        raise GeometryInputError("metric is not symmetric")
   140	    if _maximum(first - np.swapaxes(first, 1, 2)) > tolerance:
   141	        raise GeometryInputError("metric first jet is not symmetric in metric indices")
   142	    if _maximum(second - np.swapaxes(second, 0, 1)) > tolerance:
   143	        raise GeometryInputError("metric second jet is not symmetric in derivative indices")
   144	    if _maximum(second - np.swapaxes(second, 2, 3)) > tolerance:
   145	        raise GeometryInputError("metric second jet is not symmetric in metric indices")
   146	    return MetricJets(metric.copy(), first.copy(), second.copy())
   147	
   148	
   149	def evaluate_metric_jets(jets: MetricJets, tolerance: float = 2e-10) -> GeometryEvaluation:
   150	    jets = validate_metric_jets(jets, tolerance)
   151	    g, dg, ddg = jets.metric, jets.first, jets.second
   152	    try:
   153	        inverse = np.linalg.inv(g)
   154	    except np.linalg.LinAlgError as exc:
   155	        raise GeometryInputError("metric is singular") from exc
   156	    determinant = float(np.linalg.det(g))
   157	    eigenvalues = np.linalg.eigvalsh(g)
   158	    negative = int(np.count_nonzero(eigenvalues < -tolerance))
   159	    positive = int(np.count_nonzero(eigenvalues > tolerance))
   160	    zero = DIM - negative - positive
   161	    inertia = (negative, positive, zero)
   162	    if zero or sorted((negative, positive)) != [1, 3]:
   163	        raise GeometryInputError(f"metric is not Lorentzian: inertia={inertia}")
   164	
   165	    inverse_first = np.zeros((DIM, DIM, DIM))
   166	    for k in range(DIM):
   167	        inverse_first[k] = -inverse @ dg[k] @ inverse
   168	
   169	    christoffel = np.zeros((DIM, DIM, DIM))
   170	    christoffel_first = np.zeros((DIM, DIM, DIM, DIM))
   171	    for rho in range(DIM):
   172	        for mu in range(DIM):
   173	            for nu in range(DIM):
   174	                h = np.array([dg[mu, sigma, nu] + dg[nu, sigma, mu] - dg[sigma, mu, nu] for sigma in range(DIM)])
   175	                christoffel[rho, mu, nu] = 0.5 * inverse[rho] @ h
   176	                for k in range(DIM):
   177	                    dh = np.array(
   178	                        [
   179	                            ddg[k, mu, sigma, nu]
   180	                            + ddg[k, nu, sigma, mu]
   181	                            - ddg[k, sigma, mu, nu]
   182	                            for sigma in range(DIM)
   183	                        ]
   184	                    )
   185	                    christoffel_first[k, rho, mu, nu] = 0.5 * (
   186	                        inverse_first[k, rho] @ h + inverse[rho] @ dh
   187	                    )
   188	
   189	    riemann_up = np.zeros((DIM, DIM, DIM, DIM))
   190	    for rho in range(DIM):
   191	        for sigma in range(DIM):
   192	            for mu in range(DIM):
   193	                for nu in range(DIM):
   194	                    riemann_up[rho, sigma, mu, nu] = (
   195	                        christoffel_first[mu, rho, nu, sigma]
   196	                        - christoffel_first[nu, rho, mu, sigma]
   197	                        + sum(
   198	                            christoffel[rho, mu, lam] * christoffel[lam, nu, sigma]
   199	                            - christoffel[rho, nu, lam] * christoffel[lam, mu, sigma]
   200	                            for lam in range(DIM)
   201	                        )
   202	                    )
   203	    riemann_down = np.einsum("ar,rsuv->asuv", g, riemann_up)
   204	    ricci = np.einsum("rsrn->sn", riemann_up)
   205	    scalar = float(np.einsum("sn,sn", inverse, ricci))
   206	
   207	    metric_compatibility = np.zeros((DIM, DIM, DIM))
   208	    for alpha in range(DIM):
   209	        for mu in range(DIM):
   210	            for nu in range(DIM):
   211	                metric_compatibility[alpha, mu, nu] = dg[alpha, mu, nu] - sum(
   212	                    christoffel[rho, alpha, mu] * g[rho, nu]
   213	                    + christoffel[rho, alpha, nu] * g[mu, rho]
   214	                    for rho in range(DIM)
   215	                )
   216	    first_bianchi = np.zeros_like(riemann_down)
   217	    for a in range(DIM):
   218	        for b in range(DIM):
   219	            for c in range(DIM):
   220	                for d in range(DIM):
   221	                    first_bianchi[a, b, c, d] = (
   222	                        riemann_down[a, b, c, d]
   223	                        + riemann_down[a, c, d, b]
   224	                        + riemann_down[a, d, b, c]
   225	                    )
   226	
   227	    residuals = {
   228	        "inverse": _maximum(g @ inverse - np.eye(DIM)),
   229	        "christoffel_lower_symmetry": _maximum(christoffel - np.swapaxes(christoffel, 1, 2)),
   230	        "metric_compatibility": _maximum(metric_compatibility),
   231	        "riemann_last_pair_antisymmetry": _maximum(riemann_down + np.swapaxes(riemann_down, 2, 3)),
   232	        "riemann_first_pair_antisymmetry": _maximum(riemann_down + np.swapaxes(riemann_down, 0, 1)),
   233	        "riemann_pair_exchange": _maximum(riemann_down - np.transpose(riemann_down, (2, 3, 0, 1))),
   234	        "first_bianchi": _maximum(first_bianchi),
   235	        "ricci_symmetry": _maximum(ricci - ricci.T),
   236	    }
   237	    return GeometryEvaluation(
   238	        g,
   239	        inverse,
   240	        determinant,
   241	        inertia,
   242	        christoffel,
   243	        christoffel_first,
   244	        riemann_up,
   245	        riemann_down,
   246	        ricci,
   247	        scalar,
   248	        residuals,
   249	    )
   250	
   251	
   252	def metric_jets_from_coframe(
   253	    coframe,
   254	    coframe_first,
   255	    coframe_second,
   256	    eta=ETA,
   257	    tolerance: float = 2e-10,
   258	) -> MetricJets:
   259	    e = _as_float_array(coframe, (DIM, DIM), "coframe")
   260	    de = _as_float_array(coframe_first, (DIM, DIM, DIM), "coframe first jet")

   388	def metric_jets_from_split(slot_values, slot_first, slot_second, tolerance: float = 2e-10) -> MetricJets:
   389	    values = _as_float_array(slot_values, (len(SLOT_NAMES),), "slot values")
   390	    first = _as_float_array(slot_first, (DIM, len(SLOT_NAMES)), "slot first jets")
   391	    second = _as_float_array(slot_second, (DIM, DIM, len(SLOT_NAMES)), "slot second jets")
   392	    if _maximum(second - np.swapaxes(second, 0, 1)) > tolerance:
   393	        raise GeometryInputError("slot second jets are not symmetric in derivative indices")
   394	    jets = [Jet2(values[index], first[:, index], second[:, :, index]) for index in range(len(SLOT_NAMES))]

   404	            )

   428	
   429	def reconstruct_split(metric, tolerance: float = 2e-10) -> SplitReconstruction:
   430	    g = _as_float_array(metric, (DIM, DIM), "metric")
   431	    if _maximum(g - g.T) > tolerance:
   432	        raise GeometryInputError("metric is not symmetric")
   433	    screen = g[2:, 2:].copy()
   434	    try:
   435	        screen_inverse = np.linalg.inv(screen)
   436	    except np.linalg.LinAlgError as exc:
   437	        raise GeometryInputError("screen block is singular") from exc
   438	    screen_eigenvalues = np.linalg.eigvalsh(screen)
   439	    if np.any(screen_eigenvalues <= tolerance):
   440	        raise GeometryInputError("conditional screen block is not positive definite")
   441	    shifts = np.zeros((2, 2))
   442	    for i in range(2):
   443	        shifts[:, i] = screen_inverse @ g[i, 2:]
   444	    base = np.zeros((2, 2))
   445	    for i in range(2):
   446	        for j in range(2):
   447	            base[i, j] = g[i, j] - shifts[:, i] @ screen @ shifts[:, j]
   448	    slots = np.array(
   449	        [
   450	            base[0, 0], base[0, 1], base[1, 1],
   451	            screen[0, 0], screen[0, 1], screen[1, 1],
   452	            shifts[0, 0], shifts[1, 0], shifts[0, 1], shifts[1, 1],
   453	        ]
   454	    )
   455	    base_inverse = np.linalg.inv(base)
   456	    base_eigenvalues = np.linalg.eigvalsh(base)
   457	    if not (base_eigenvalues[0] < -tolerance and base_eigenvalues[1] > tolerance):
   458	        raise GeometryInputError("conditional base block is not Lorentzian")
   459	    block_inverse = np.zeros((DIM, DIM))
   460	    block_inverse[:2, :2] = base_inverse
   461	    block_inverse[:2, 2:] = -base_inverse @ shifts.T
   462	    block_inverse[2:, :2] = -shifts @ base_inverse
   463	    block_inverse[2:, 2:] = screen_inverse + shifts @ base_inverse @ shifts.T
   464	    determinant_factor = float(np.linalg.det(base) * np.linalg.det(screen))
   465	    rebuilt = metric_jets_from_split(slots, np.zeros((DIM, 10)), np.zeros((DIM, DIM, 10))).metric
   466	    residuals = {
   467	        "forward_reverse": _maximum(rebuilt - g),
   468	        "block_inverse": _maximum(block_inverse - np.linalg.inv(g)),
   469	        "determinant_factorization": abs(determinant_factor - float(np.linalg.det(g))),
   470	    }
   471	    return SplitReconstruction(slots, base, screen, shifts, block_inverse, determinant_factor, residuals)
   472	
   473	
   474	def csn_scaled_metric_jets(jets: MetricJets, omega: float, sigma_first, sigma_second) -> MetricJets:
   475	    jets = validate_metric_jets(jets)
   476	    if not np.isfinite(omega) or omega <= 0:
   477	        raise GeometryInputError("CSN factor must be finite and positive")
   478	    sigma = _as_float_array(sigma_first, (DIM,), "d ln Omega")
   479	    dsigma = _as_float_array(sigma_second, (DIM, DIM), "dd ln Omega")
   480	    if _maximum(dsigma - dsigma.T) > 2e-10:
   481	        raise GeometryInputError("dd ln Omega is not symmetric")
   482	    scale = omega**2
   483	    g = scale * jets.metric
   484	    dg = np.zeros_like(jets.first)
   485	    ddg = np.zeros_like(jets.second)
   486	    for a in range(DIM):
   487	        dg[a] = scale * (jets.first[a] + 2.0 * sigma[a] * jets.metric)
   488	        for b in range(DIM):
   489	            ddg[a, b] = scale * (
   490	                jets.second[a, b]
   491	                + 2.0 * sigma[b] * jets.first[a]
   492	                + 2.0 * sigma[a] * jets.first[b]
   493	                + (2.0 * dsigma[a, b] + 4.0 * sigma[a] * sigma[b]) * jets.metric
   494	            )
   495	    return validate_metric_jets(MetricJets(g, dg, ddg))

ETA=np.diag([-1.,1.,1.,1.])
def rel(a,b):
 a=np.asarray(a);b=np.asarray(b);return np.max(np.abs(a-b))/max(1.,np.max(np.abs(b)))
def trmetric(g,dg,ddg,J):
 return (np.einsum('ma,mn,nb->ab',J,g,J),np.einsum('ka,mb,nc,kmn->abc',J,J,J,dg),np.einsum('ka,lb,mc,nd,klmn->abcd',J,J,J,J,ddg))
def trfour(R,J):return np.einsum('ra,sb,uc,vd,rsuv->abcd',J,J,J,J,R)
def direct_R(g,dg,ddg):
 gi=np.linalg.inv(g); dgi=np.array([-gi@dg[k]@gi for k in range(4)])
 G=np.zeros((4,4,4));dG=np.zeros((4,4,4,4))
 for r in range(4):
  for m in range(4):
   for n in range(4):
    H=np.array([dg[m,s,n]+dg[n,s,m]-dg[s,m,n] for s in range(4)])
    G[r,m,n]=.5*gi[r]@H
    for k in range(4):
     dH=np.array([ddg[k,m,s,n]+ddg[k,n,s,m]-ddg[k,s,m,n] for s in range(4)])
     dG[k,r,m,n]=.5*(dgi[k,r]@H+gi[r]@dH)
 Rup=np.zeros((4,4,4,4))
 for r in range(4):
  for s in range(4):
   for m in range(4):
    for n in range(4):
     Rup[r,s,m,n]=dG[m,r,n,s]-dG[n,r,m,s]+sum(G[r,m,l]*G[l,n,s]-G[r,n,l]*G[l,m,s] for l in range(4))
 return np.einsum('ar,rsuv->asuv',g,Rup)
def cartan(e,g,R):
 Rup=np.einsum('ra,asuv->rsuv',np.linalg.inv(g),R)
 return np.einsum('ir,rsuv,sj->ijuv',e,Rup,np.linalg.inv(e))
def gen(name):
 K=np.zeros((4,4))
 if name=='K01':K[0,1]=K[1,0]=1
 elif name=='K02':K[0,2]=K[2,0]=1
 else:K[2,3]=-1;K[3,2]=1
 return K

for x in reg:x['J']=np.array(json.loads(x['matrix_json']))

 for i in range(4):lor1=max(lor1,rel(dL[i].T@ETA@L+L.T@ETA@dL[i],np.zeros((4,4))))

  for line in f:
   z=json.loads(line);nraw+=1
   g=np.array(z['metric']);dg=np.array(z['metric_first']);ddg=np.array(z['metric_second']);e=np.array(z['coframe']);de=np.array(z['coframe_first']);dde=np.array(z['coframe_second']);R=np.array(z['riemann_down'])

     metric2=max(metric2,rel(gr,g),rel(dgr,dg),rel(ddgr,ddg));nmetric+=1

    10	## Result first
    11	
    12	The complete registered atlas separates two things that the earlier ensemble map left entangled:
    13	
    14	1. The full metric/curvature interaction structure is invariant under every registered invertible
    15	   chart and Lorentz-coframe transformation. Component values and singular values change, but every
    16	   full-tensor activity decision and every full-tensor interaction span rank is unchanged.
    17	2. The slot/shear/twist account is invariant only while the same supplied 2+2 distributions are
    18	   retained. If a chart mixes or re-seats which coordinate directions are called base and screen,
    19	   those split diagnostics can acquire many new Möbius terms without any change in the underlying
    20	   tensor geometry.
    21	
    22	That is not a new mechanism. It is a clean representation/partition distinction.
    23

    25	
    26	- Parent configurations: 6,144 = 48 carriers x 16 masks x 8 contexts.

   238	    check("inverse_cross", relmax(transforms["C03_CROSS_GENERAL"]["matrix"] @ transforms["C04_CROSS_GENERAL_INVERSE"]["matrix"], np.eye(4)) <= TOL)

   241	    check("configuration_shards", len(config_shards) == 12 and sum(int(r["rows"]) for r in config_shards) == 73728)
   242	    check("mobius_shards", len(mobius_shards) == 12 and sum(int(r["rows"]) for r in mobius_shards) == 69120)
   243	    for shard in config_shards + mobius_shards:
   244	        check(f"shard_hash_{shard['transform_id']}_{shard['path']}", digest(HERE / shard["path"]) == shard["sha256"])

   276	            for name in SPLIT_PAYLOADS:

   279	                else:

   281	    check("mobius_unique_total", len(interaction_lookup) == 69120)
   282

   301	    split_forward_residual = 0.0

   303	    local_anchor_count = 0
   304	    split_source_count = 0

   310	            g, dg, ddg = (np.asarray(raw[x], dtype=float) for x in ("metric", "metric_first", "metric_second"))
   311	            e, de, dde = (np.asarray(raw[x], dtype=float) for x in ("coframe", "coframe_first", "coframe_second"))
   312	            if mask in {0, 15}:
   313	                for identity, item in transforms.items():
   314	                    if item["kind"] == "COFRAME":
   315	                        lam = item["matrix"]
   316	                        first = np.asarray(json.loads(item["parameter_first_json"]), dtype=float)
   317	                        second = np.asarray(json.loads(item["parameter_second_json"]), dtype=float)
   318	                        k = generator(item["generator"])
   319	                        dlam = np.array([first[a] * k @ lam for a in range(4)])
   320	                        ddlam = np.array([[second[a, b] * k @ lam + first[a] * first[b] * k @ k @ lam for b in range(4)] for a in range(4)])
   321	                        et = lam @ e
   322	                        det = np.array([dlam[a] @ e + lam @ de[a] for a in range(4)])
   323	                        ddet = np.array([[ddlam[a, b] @ e + dlam[a] @ de[b] + dlam[b] @ de[a] + lam @ dde[a, b] for b in range(4)] for a in range(4)])
   324	                        rebuilt = coframe_metric(et, det, ddet)
   325	                        local_metric_residual = max(local_metric_residual, relmax(rebuilt[0], g), relmax(rebuilt[1], dg), relmax(rebuilt[2], ddg))
   326	                        local_anchor_count += 1
   327	                if raw["carrier_id"] == "R00_1":

   329	                        if item["kind"] != "COORDINATE":

   371	                        else:
   372	                            vector = sum(((-1) ** (target.bit_count() - s.bit_count())) * vertices[index] for index, s in enumerate(subsets))
   373	                            split_interaction_residual = max(split_interaction_residual, abs(float(saved[f"{name}_l2"]) - float(np.linalg.norm(vector))) / max(1.0, float(np.linalg.norm(vector))), abs(float(saved[f"{name}_max_abs"]) - float(np.max(np.abs(vector)))) / max(1.0, float(np.max(np.abs(vector)))))
   374	                        split_interaction_checks += 1
   375	    check("split_interaction_check_count", split_interaction_checks == 4 * 8 * 2 * 4 * 3)
   376	    check("split_interactions_independent", split_interaction_residual <= TOL)

# Chart/Coframe Invariance Atlas — Preregistration

Date: 2026-07-21

Branch: `codex/udt-chart-coframe-invariance-atlas-2026-07-21`

Parent commit: `ba572f589eae83c9f74de1b93b34d389529b27b7`

## Whole question

For the complete 6,144-configuration structural-ensemble atlas already banked at the parent commit,
which recorded structures are unchanged tensor geometry, which merely change components under an
invertible chart or Lorentz coframe transformation, which depend on the supplied coordinate 2+2
partition, and which become undefined when that supplied partition leaves its admitted signature
domain?

This is a bounded invariance atlas. It does not select a chart, coframe, partition, action, source,
carrier, boundary condition, or desired physical branch.

## Mode and scope

- Method order: `MAP -> OBSERVE -> PONDER -> DERIVE`.
- Question type: metric-led representation and supplied-partition audit.
- Compute: CPU-only algebra over saved configuration jets. No relaxation, fitting, GPU work, or new
  solution search.
- Parent configuration universe: all 48 carriers, all 16 ensemble masks, and all 8 contexts,
  totaling 6,144 configurations.
- Parent interaction universe: all 48 carriers, all 15 nonempty ensemble subsets, and all 8
  contexts, totaling 5,760 Möbius targets per transformation.
- Transformation universe: the twelve transformations fixed below. Therefore the required coverage
  is 73,728 configuration-orbit rows and 69,120 interaction-orbit rows.
- Every transformation/configuration and transformation/interaction combination is retained.
  Invalid or marginal supplied splits are outcomes, not grounds for exclusion.

## Frozen source evidence

The build must verify these manifests before reading outcomes:

| source | required manifest SHA-256 |
|---|---|
| `udt_structural_ensemble_metric_atlas_2026-07-21/SHA256SUMS.txt` | `3d569ed31506f5f7ce44beac30e8419571f734b3973dcc34d6c474bf78636757` |
| `udt_canonical_geometry_evaluator_p01_2026-07-21/SHA256SUMS.txt` | `b7d61760e3ac3dc9dc2a51a7a505f02dad964fe8d7dfc1f1ed8df3cc3eb1b543` |
| `udt_complete_metric_solution_space_map_2026-07-21/SHA256SUMS.txt` | `17780f41355121df4ecf86bd81606ef597cc6f5f26d90c0e443a5d2eac24d13a` |

The parent raw shards, registries, and Möbius ledger are immutable inputs. This package may not
rewrite them.

## Fixed transformation registry

### Constant coordinate charts

Convention: `x = J x'`; covariant coordinate indices therefore acquire a right factor `J`. All
matrices are constant, invertible probes.

1. `C00_IDENTITY`: `J = I4`.
2. `C01_BLOCK_GENERAL`:

   ```text
   [[1, .2, 0, 0], [.1, 1, 0, 0],
    [0, 0, 1, -.15], [0, 0, .25, 1]]
   ```

3. `C02_BLOCK_GENERAL_INVERSE`: the mathematical inverse of `C01_BLOCK_GENERAL`.
4. `C03_CROSS_GENERAL`:

   ```text
   [[1, 0, .12, 0], [0, 1, 0, -.18],
    [.07, 0, 1, 0], [0, .09, 0, 1]]
   ```

5. `C04_CROSS_GENERAL_INVERSE`: the mathematical inverse of `C03_CROSS_GENERAL`.
6. `C05_SWAP_DEPTH_SCREEN`: permutation exchanging coordinate indices 1 and 2.
7. `C06_SWAP_TIME_SCREEN`: permutation exchanging coordinate indices 0 and 2.

`C01/C02` preserve the supplied base/screen distributions. `C03/C04` mix them while retaining the
new first-two/last-two coordinate split as an independently reported supplied split. `C05/C06`
re-seat that supplied split. A split invalidated by signature is still retained and classified.

### Internal Lorentz coframes

Convention: `e' = Lambda e`, with internal signature `diag(-1,1,1,1)`. A boost generator `K0a` has
`K[0,a] = K[a,0] = 1`. The screen-rotation generator has `K[2,3] = -1`, `K[3,2] = 1`.

1. `F01_CONSTANT_BASE_BOOST`: `exp(.31 K01)`.
2. `F02_LOCAL_BASE_BOOST`: `exp(theta K01)` with, at the sampled point,
   `theta=.31`, gradient `[.07,-.04,.03,.05]`, and Hessian

   ```text
   [[.02,.01,0,-.005], [.01,-.015,.004,0],
    [0,.004,.01,.006], [-.005,0,.006,-.012]]
   ```

3. `F03_CONSTANT_CROSS_BOOST`: `exp(.27 K02)`.
4. `F04_LOCAL_CROSS_BOOST`: `exp(theta K02)` with `theta=-.22`, gradient
   `[-.03,.06,.02,-.05]`, and Hessian

   ```text
   [[.011,-.004,.003,0], [-.004,.018,0,-.006],
    [.003,0,-.009,.005], [0,-.006,.005,.014]]
   ```

5. `F05_LOCAL_SCREEN_ROTATION`: `exp(theta K23)` with `theta=.37`, gradient
   `[.04,.02,-.06,.03]`, and Hessian

   ```text
   [[-.008,.003,0,.004], [.003,.012,-.005,0],
    [0,-.005,.016,.002], [.004,0,.002,-.011]]
   ```

Local first and second coframe jets must include the registered derivatives of `Lambda`; metric
jets must nevertheless remain unchanged. No Lorentz coframe map redefines the coordinate split.

## Payloads and classifications

For every configuration the atlas records:

- metric, first and second metric jets;
- Riemann, Weyl, Ricci, scalar curvature, and metric determinant/inertia;
- Cartan curvature in the internal coframe;
- scalar-field value, gradient, and Hessian;
- supplied-split validity, inverse/reconstruction residual, slot jets, shear, and twist whenever
  the transformed split is admitted.

For every interaction cube it recomputes the exact four-ensemble Möbius interaction for:

- metric two-jet;
- Riemann, Weyl, Ricci, and scalar curvature;
- Cartan curvature;
- scalar-field two-jet;
- supplied-split slot two-jet, shear, and twist when all required vertices admit that split.

Each row receives exactly one primary status:

- `TENSOR_COVARIANT_COMPONENT_CHANGE`;
- `METRIC_INVARIANT_COFRAME_GAUGE`;
- `SUPPLIED_SPLIT_RESEATED_DEFINED`;
- `SUPPLIED_SPLIT_UNDEFINED_SIGNATURE`;
- `SUPPLIED_SPLIT_MARGINAL`;
- `NUMERIC_COVARIANCE_FAILURE`.

Tensor geometry and supplied-split diagnostics must be reported on separate axes. A coordinate
change is never counted as a new geometry. A newly re-seated first-two/last-two split is not silently
identified with the push-forward of the original distributions.

## Premise ledger

| item | tag | scope/source |
|---|---|---|
| Four-dimensional conformal-Lorentzian coframe/metric | `pinned-by-THEORY`, conditional realization | parent complete-metric map and canonical evaluator |
| Existing 48 x 16 x 8 jet universe | `pinned-by-EVIDENCE` | parent ensemble atlas |
| Exact twelve finite transformations | `free-and-explored` | bounded probes fixed above before outcomes |
| Constant coordinate transformations only | `free-and-explored` limitation | nonlinear charts are not covered |
| Lorentz internal coframe transformations | `pinned-by-THEORY` as metric redundancy | parent redundancy ledger G01/G02 |
| Coordinate diffeomorphism representation equivalence | `pinned-by-THEORY` as representation redundancy | parent redundancy ledger G03 |
| First-two/last-two 2+2 split | `CHOSE`, conditional | parent realization G06; audited rather than promoted |
| Ensemble identity attached to parent histories | `CHOSE` | masks are transformed after construction; they are not re-fit or re-parameterized |
| Absolute component activity threshold `1e-9` | `pinned-by-HABIT`, inherited numeric rule | parent ensemble atlas; margins must be reported |
| Split eigenvalue/signature tolerance `1e-9` | `pinned-by-HABIT` | numeric classification only |
| Relative covariance/reconstruction tolerance `1e-10` | `pinned-by-HABIT` | certification gate |
| Action, source, carrier, section, boundary, physical scale | `OPEN` and not sampled | outside atlas |

## Certification and falsification contract

The build fails closed unless:

1. all frozen input manifests match;
2. all 6,144 parent configurations and 5,760 parent interactions are accounted for;
3. all 73,728 configuration and 69,120 interaction transformation rows exist uniquely;
4. every registered `J` is invertible and every registered `Lambda` preserves the internal metric;
5. `C01/C02` and `C03/C04` round trips have relative error at most `1e-10`;
6. metric, curvature, scalar, and Cartan covariance residuals are at most `1e-10`, otherwise the row
   is retained as `NUMERIC_COVARIANCE_FAILURE` and the atlas cannot certify invariance;
7. local Lorentz coframe jets reproduce unchanged metric two-jets to `1e-10` on an independently
   fixed anchor set containing every carrier/context pair and both empty/full masks;
8. every admitted transformed split reconstructs the transformed metric two-jet to `1e-10`;
9. no undefined or marginal split is imputed, discarded, or included in a defined-only span rank;
10. Möbius tensors agree with the corresponding linear tensor representation to `1e-10` wherever
    that comparison is defined;
11. activity-concordance and span-rank statements include threshold margins and defined-row counts;
12. a fresh independent verifier recomputes the load-bearing transformation and split algebra without
    importing the atlas builder.

Required exercised catch-proofs must reject a missing transformation row, duplicate row, singular
chart, non-Lorentz coframe, wrong inverse pairing, omitted local-Lorentz derivative, tensor-index
permutation error, invalid split silently treated as valid, undefined split imputation, mutated parent
input, altered ensemble mask, Möbius cube omission, threshold-margin omission, and claim escalation.

## Required outputs

- deterministic builder and independent verifier;
- exact transformation registry;
- one configuration-orbit shard and one Möbius-orbit shard per transformation;
- shard registries with row counts and SHA-256 values;
- aggregate invariance, split-domain, interaction-order, span-rank, and numeric-margin censuses;
- premise/status ledgers, anti-imposition audit, machine-readable result, transcripts, commands,
  repository gates, manifest, technical audit report, lay report, and next-decision record.

Compact transformed ledgers are permitted instead of duplicating full transformed tensor arrays,
because each transformed tensor is deterministically reconstructible from the immutable parent raw
jets plus the exact transformation registry. The compact rows must retain the transform, object,
status, norms, residuals, activity, split-domain status, and source identity needed to reproduce every
aggregate.

## Maximum allowed conclusion

`BOUNDED_CHART_COFRAME_AND_SUPPLIED_SPLIT_INVARIANCE_ATLAS_CHARACTERIZED`

The atlas may classify invariant tensor content, component dependence, coframe gauge behavior, and
supplied-partition dependence within the registered finite transformation set. It may not claim a
globally selected chart, coframe, 2+2 split, carrier, boundary, action, matter law, physical universe,
or proof over the full diffeomorphism/Lorentz groups.

# Verdict: FAIL

The bounded mathematical conclusion is supported, but the package cannot be certified as `COMPLETE_VERIFIED_WITH_CAVEATS` in its present form. The failures concern evidence completeness and claimed independence—not a counterexample to the geometry.

## Decisive failures

1. **The banked package is incomplete and not reproducible as delivered.**

   - `PREREGISTRATION.md` and `PREREGISTRATION_CORRECTION.md` are listed in [SOURCE_LINEAGE.tsv](/tmp/udt_startup_rehearsal_20260719_h0zjlA/repo/udt_chart_coframe_invariance_atlas_2026-07-21/SOURCE_LINEAGE.tsv:5) but absent from the package directory. Their exact hashes do exist in Git commits `f572769` and `fefa380`, so preregistration itself is genuine.
   - [COMMANDS.md](/tmp/udt_startup_rehearsal_20260719_h0zjlA/repo/udt_chart_coframe_invariance_atlas_2026-07-21/COMMANDS.md:10) claims execution of `build_manifest.py` and `verify_repository_gates.py`, but neither script nor `SHA256SUMS.txt` is present.
   - The verifier therefore cannot replay on the mandated `grok` worktree. It presently stops at the absent parent source; after restoring that source, it would next stop at the absent preregistration files required at [verify_invariance_atlas.py](/tmp/udt_startup_rehearsal_20260719_h0zjlA/repo/udt_chart_coframe_invariance_atlas_2026-07-21/verify_invariance_atlas.py:225).

2. **Independent verification is overstated.**

   - The verifier checks builder-produced Cartan residual columns at [verify_invariance_atlas.py](/tmp/udt_startup_rehearsal_20260719_h0zjlA/repo/udt_chart_coframe_invariance_atlas_2026-07-21/verify_invariance_atlas.py:257), but its independent raw recomputation block covers metric jets, coordinate Riemann curvature, and split reconstruction—not Cartan curvature ([line 295](/tmp/udt_startup_rehearsal_20260719_h0zjlA/repo/udt_chart_coframe_invariance_atlas_2026-07-21/verify_invariance_atlas.py:295)).
   - The `D2` reconstruction is meaningfully separate for Schur-complement jet algebra, but shares the canonical forward evaluator and nearly identical shear/twist formulas. It detects many builder implementation mistakes, not a shared convention or kinematics error.
   - Several advertised catch-proofs are synthetic false predicates rather than exercised mutations: K06 only removes a JSON vector and checks its length; K07 adds `1e-3` to an already computed residual; K10 compares a dummy zero hash ([lines 393–399](/tmp/udt_startup_rehearsal_20260719_h0zjlA/repo/udt_chart_coframe_invariance_atlas_2026-07-21/verify_invariance_atlas.py:393)). These do not prove that the full verification path catches the named faults.

3. **One rank-threshold caveat is omitted.**

   C05/M4 `split_slot_twojet` rank 130 retains a singular value of `1.0766158328e-9` while discarding `3.3477070080e-10` at the `1e-9` threshold ([exact row](/tmp/udt_startup_rehearsal_20260719_h0zjlA/repo/udt_chart_coframe_invariance_atlas_2026-07-21/TRANSFORMED_SPAN_RANKS.tsv:789)). The report discusses activity margins at [AUDIT_REPORT.md](/tmp/udt_startup_rehearsal_20260719_h0zjlA/repo/udt_chart_coframe_invariance_atlas_2026-07-21/AUDIT_REPORT.md:107), but not this rank sensitivity.
